									<p>Getting a healthy, pedigree Labrador puppy requires planning. 				<section data-wpr-lazyrender="1" class="penci-section penci-disSticky penci-structure-10 elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-fe54c0d elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="fe54c0d" data-element_type="section" data-e-type="section" data-settings='{"background_background":"classic"}'>
						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="penci-ercol-100 penci-ercol-order-1 penci-sticky-ct  elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-db340da" data-id="db340da" data-element_type="column" data-e-type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<section class="penci-section penci-disSticky penci-structure-32 elementor-section elementor-inner-section elementor-element elementor-element-4be11719 elementor-section-content-middle elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="4be11719" data-element_type="section" data-e-type="section">
						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-no">
					<div class="penci-ercol-50 penci-ercol-order-1 penci-sticky-ct  elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-e908e6c" data-id="e908e6c" data-element_type="column" data-e-type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-578c7719 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="578c7719" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Labrador Puppy Care</h2>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2bf34783 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="2bf34783" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
									<p>Build his/her routine care into your schedule to help your Lab live longer, stay healthier, and be happier during his/her lifetime. We cannot overemphasize the importance of a proper diet and exercise routine.</p>								</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-10032a86 elementor-icon-list--layout-traditional elementor-list-item-link-full_width elementor-widget elementor-widget-icon-list" data-id="10032a86" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="icon-list.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
							<ul class="elementor-icon-list-items">
							<li class="elementor-icon-list-item">
											<span class="elementor-icon-list-icon">
							<i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-bone"></i>						</span>
										<span class="elementor-icon-list-text">Brush his/her coat as needed, at least weekly.</span>
									</li>
								<li class="elementor-icon-list-item">
											<span class="elementor-icon-list-icon">
							<i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-bone"></i>						</span>
										<span class="elementor-icon-list-text">Clean her/his ears weekly, even as a puppy.</span>
									</li>
								<li class="elementor-icon-list-item">
											<span class="elementor-icon-list-icon">
							<i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-bone"></i>						</span>
										<span class="elementor-icon-list-text">Keep your dog&rsquo;s diet consistent and don&rsquo;t give her people food.</span>
									</li>
								<li class="elementor-icon-list-item">
											<span class="elementor-icon-list-icon">
							<i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-bone"></i>						</span>
										<span class="elementor-icon-list-text">Feed a high-quality diet appropriate for her age.</span>
									</li>
								<li class="elementor-icon-list-item">
											<span class="elementor-icon-list-icon">
							<i aria-hidden="true" class="fas fa-bone"></i>						</span>
										<span class="elementor-icon-list-text">Exercise your dog regularly, but don&rsquo;t overdo it at first.</span>
									</li>
						</ul>
						</div>
				</div>
					</div>
		</div>

												<a class="elementor-accordion-title" tabindex="0">How much is a Labrador Retriever ?</a>

												<a class="elementor-accordion-title" tabindex="0">How to Groom a Labrador Retriever?</a>

Combining them every day during heavy shedding and bathing in warm water removes the dead hair. Use a good shampoo, then rinse with clean, not hot, water.</p></div>

However, according to a recent study, Chocolate Labs live shorter lives than black and yellow Labradors, averaging 10.7 years versus 14 years. 												<a class="elementor-accordion-title" tabindex="0">How much Food to Feed a Labrador Retriever ?</a>
					</div>
					<div id="elementor-tab-content-3587" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="7" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-3587"><p>There is no one answer to how much food your dog should eat. Some people recommend 3 cups of food for a 50-pound Labrador, but you will need more if your dog is bigger than that. You need to know what kind of food they can eat, so check the Labrador puppy feeding chart on most foods before you buy one. If you notice that your dog is getting fat, go to the doctor. Your veterinarian has all of the history on him and can offer suggestions. If he eats too much food even though you are feeding him enough, it might be because he is not hungry anymore.</p></div>

In practice, there is a vast range of hues of <a class="wpil_keyword_link " href="https://labradortime.com/yellow-labrador-retrievers/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" title="yellow Labrador" data-wpil-keyword-link="linked">yellow Labrador</a> color, from palest cream to deepest fox red.</p></div>
